wiki-backgroundcolor-light\">Upcoming Matches</div></div></div></div>\n<p><b>RLCS 2021-22</b> is the second <a href=\"/rocketleague/RLCS\" class=\"mw-redirect\" title=\"RLCS\">RLCS</a> season in 2021, crossing over into 2022. This season introduces the most major changes to the RLCS system yet with more regions and an updated format. 3 splits - Fall, Winter, Spring - each have 3 regional events leading into an international major. Within all these events, each team collects points that will determine whether they will qualify for the World Championship or World Championship Wildcard.\n</p>\n<div id=\"toc\" class=\"toc\" href=\"/rocketleague/index.php?title=Rocket_League_Championship_Series/2021-22/Spring/North_America/1&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9\" title=\"Edit section: Format\">edit</a><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>Double Elimination Bracket.\n<ul><li>Upper Bracket: Round 1 and Quarterfinals are <abbr title=\"Best of 5\">Bo5</abbr>. Semifinals and Finals are <abbr title=\"Best of 7\">Bo7</abbr>.</li>\n<li>Lower Bracket: Round 1, 2 and 3 are <abbr title=\"Best of 5\">Bo5</abbr>. Quarterfinals, Semifinals and Finals are <abbr title=\"Best of 7\">Bo7</abbr>.</li>\n<li>Grand Finals are <abbr title=\"Best of 7\">Bo7</abbr> with a Bracket Reset, where the team coming from the Lower Finals must win 2 <abbr title=\"Best of 7\">Bo7</abbr> series.</li></ul></li></ul>\n<h3><span class=\"mw-headline\" id=\"Prize_Pool\">Prize Pool</span><span class=\"mw-editsection\"><span
